Commentary

The Future of Anglo-American Cooperation 24

— Heng

Regarding the issue of naval reduction, I sincerely hope for Anglo-American cooperation. I have already discussed this in detail in previous articles. According to recent foreign dispatches, there is already a tendency in this direction in the attitudes of British and American authorities. For example, Stanley Baldwin, the leader of the British Conservative Party, on the one hand, hopes that the United States will join the League of Nations soon; on the other hand, he advocates that the actions of the British Navy should be shifted in accordance with the attitude of the United States. The implication is that Britain's wavering attitude today is actually influenced by the United States. At the same time, the British Foreign Office has formally denied the rumors of a non-aggression treaty between Britain and Japan. As for Washington, it has repeatedly expressed its views on this point in recent days, and Secretary of State Cordell Hull's conversation with reporters is particularly clear. Judging from this, the Anglo-American cooperation that we have been hoping for has now begun to show its signs. If Japan is determined to abolish the treaty, Britain and the United States, in order to maintain the balance of power in the Far East, will have no choice but to cooperate.

For a month, the ambiguous attitude of Britain has made the trend of naval reduction talks obscure and difficult to understand. However, as of today, the attitudes of Britain, the United States, and Japan towards naval reduction have become clear again. Japan's position is entirely based on equality of armaments, while the attitudes of Britain and the United States are still to maintain the Washington Naval Treaty. Britain's ambiguous attitude before, without immediately expressing a clear position, was probably intended to determine the true intentions of the United States and Japan in order to prepare to determine its own policy. Now, judging from Baldwin's words, we know that if the United States can truly be unyielding towards Japan and prepare to maintain the naval treaty by force, then the British Navy will also cooperate with the United States. From this, we can judge that the British attitude towards Japan in the past was mostly of a "hypocritical" nature and not truly affectionate towards Japan.

Now that the attitudes of Britain and the United States have gradually become clear, the future development will naturally be nothing more than two paths: (1) Japan yields and makes concessions; (2) Japan refuses to yield and resolutely resists the pressure from Britain and the United States. According to yesterday's Dongdian observations, Japan's abolition of the Washington Naval Treaty will not change slightly due to the joint opposition of Britain and the United States. The policy it has adopted is already very clear. In other words, Japan is already prepared to resist the joint pressure from Britain and the United States.

Given the development of the naval reduction negotiations, there are several things that the Chinese people should pay attention to: (1) The significance of Anglo-American cooperation for our country; (2) The time frame for Britain and the United States to exert real pressure on Japan; (3) Our country's preparations. Some Chinese people believe that Anglo-American cooperation is extremely good news, thinking that all of Japan's aggressive actions against us can be corrected by this. Others believe that Anglo-American cooperation is purely for their own benefit, and if Japan were to submit, the pressure from Britain and the United States on us might not be different from that of Japan. Both of these attitudes seem excessive. The former is overly optimistic, and the latter is too pessimistic. In fact, if Britain and the United States can truly cooperate to exert real pressure on Japan, no matter what, it can at least slightly curb the ambitions of militarism. Moreover, Britain and the United States themselves have contradictions and opposing points, making it difficult to be consistent everywhere.

As for the timing of exerting real pressure on Japan and our future preparations, there is also a close relationship. Based on the situation, it will take at least five years. The reasons for this are as follows: (1) The disputes in Europe have become increasingly complex since the Marseille Massacre. It is impossible to resolve the European situation in the short term. If the European situation is not settled, the British Navy cannot boldly move east to support the American fleet. (2) The British Singapore naval base must be completed by the end of 1938. (3) The American Vinson Naval Construction Plan must also be completed in 1939. (4) After declaring the abolition of the treaty, Japan will also do its best to build warships in response to future events. Therefore, in the short term, Britain's ability to intervene in Far Eastern affairs is still constrained, and the American Navy also needs to be expanded. All of this is clearly visible in the situation.

Anglo-American Real Pressure on Japan Cannot Be Realized Immediately.

As mentioned above, we must be prepared for the arrival of this event. A country on earth must first have its own way of survival before it can talk about taking advantage of the diplomatic situation. Therefore, today's national defense should be arranged with all our strength. As for international assistance, it is secondary.

Philippine National Defense Plan 25

Cultivating Aviation Talents and Organizing the Army

Complete Independence in Fourteen Years

[Manila] Filipinos anticipate that a republican government will soon be established and complete independence will be obtained. They are now engaged in a national defense plan in preparation for the implementation of the independence plan and to obtain the necessary guarantees. The Constitutional Assembly, which closed on November 8, passed a bill stipulating the establishment of a National Defense Bureau. The parliament also stipulated an increase in police force and the establishment of a police air defense force as the basis for the future organization of the army on the island. This plan will be accepted by Philippine Governor-General Murphy. After its approval, it will become law. The National Defense Act stipulates an implementation fund of 102,800 yuan and stipulates that students will be sent to the U.S. Army School for study. A total of 20 people will be sent to West Point, 12 to Annapolis, and 12 to other flight schools. The plan sets a 14-year plan with a total cost of 2 million yuan. It is estimated that when the island becomes fully independent in 14 years, there will be 420 Philippine military officers with military knowledge to lead the Philippine army. In addition, there are 6,500 officers and men of the Philippine Detective Team and the Philippine Police Supplementary Detective Team, and 6,000 policemen. Another bill allocates 512,500 yuan to expand the police force, adding 1,800 policemen and police officers. The police expenses stipulated in the budget are 1,750,000 yuan. In addition, 250,000 yuan is designated as the cost of a police air force of ten aircraft and 120 pilots. There is currently no air force in the police, and there are very few police officers with flight experience. (November 26, National Electric)

Details of Sino-Soviet-Japanese Negotiations on the Sale and Purchase of the Chinese Eastern Railway 26

Still No Results

[Tokyo] Soviet Ambassador Yurenev met with Foreign Minister Hirota at 2:00 p.m. on the 26th. The meeting lasted for five hours. Based on new instructions, the Soviet Ambassador put forward a comprehensive plan for various outstanding issues on detailed conditions, and continued the previous negotiations on issues such as payment methods and acceptance, but no expected progress was made. They agreed to study again and then left at about 7:00 p.m. (November 26, Japanese United Electric)

Tokyo Soviet Ambassador Yurenev received a reply from the Moscow government regarding the guarantee of payment and the method of assessing the payment of materials in the Sino-Soviet Eastern Railway transfer negotiations. He visited Foreign Minister Hirota at 2:00 p.m. today and discussed the details based on this reply. It is expected that the Soviet side will make some concessions in this meeting. (November 26, Dentsu Electric)

Britain Solemnly Declares to Japan to Preserve China's Territory 27

A Clear Expression After Anglo-American Understanding

Political Issues Definitely Raised in Naval Talks

[London] According to reliable sources today, British Foreign Secretary Simon has solemnly declared to Japanese Ambassador Matsudaira and Japanese naval representative Yamamoto that issues such as China's territorial integrity should be taken into consideration at all times. This is the basis of Britain's Far Eastern policy and cannot be separated. The British Foreign Secretary has notified Japan in firm and clear terms. Observers here believe that the British Foreign Office's re-declaration of its policy is the result of the recent Anglo-American understanding, and it is also heard that American envoy Davis will also advise Ambassador Matsudaira on the U.S. government's concern for maintaining the open door policy and continuing to recognize China's territorial integrity, and China's concerns have also been dispelled by Foreign Secretary Simon's statement. (November 25, National Electric)

[London] When Foreign Secretary Simon met with Ambassador Matsudaira on the 21st, he raised the issue of China, saying that preserving China's territory is the foundation of Britain's Far Eastern policy and must not be changed. This policy was also stated during the Anglo-American talks on the 23rd and was endorsed by the United States. The U.S. will raise the issue of China's open door and territorial integrity, which are of utmost concern to the U.S., at the next U.S.-Japan talks. The reason why Britain and the United States have raised the issue of China is to reject Japan's request for equality. The trend is extremely noteworthy. (November 25, Dentsu Electric)

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon announced in the House of Commons today that Japan has replied to Britain's protest against the oil monopoly in "Manchukuo" and has now ordered Ambassador Clive to reply. The British government is closely watching the issue but cannot make further announcements at this time. The Foreign Secretary denied the claim that Britain is acting alone on the matter and said that it is in close contact with the United States and the Netherlands. (November 26, Reuters Electric)

US-Japan Talks on the Situation After Treaty Abandonment 28

Japanese Side Denies Mentioning 5·4·4 Ratio

[London] During the meeting between the US General Representative Davis and the Japanese Ambassador Matsudaira this morning, they discussed the possible procedures for holding naval talks after Japan abolished the Washington Naval Treaty. This morning's meeting was the first informal discussion between the two countries' General Representatives. It is now expected that Japan will announce the abolition of the Washington Treaty on December 10. Some parties now feel that the abolition of the treaty will bring the naval talks to an end. It is heard that political issues were not mentioned during this morning's meeting, because Matsudaira stated that Japan's reply to the questions raised by Britain two weeks ago was not yet complete. These questions involve qualitative restrictions on naval forces, the non-construction of defensive works in territories in the Pacific, and mutual notification of warship construction procedures. According to Matsudaira, he is still awaiting instructions from the government regarding the non-construction of defensive works in territories in the Pacific. Matsudaira officially assured Davis that there is no basis for the rumor that Japan proposed a 5·4·4 ratio for the navy to Britain. People in London now feel that if the naval talks turn to political aspects, Japan will definitely be asked about China's territorial integrity and the open door. However, this question will not be raised until Matsudaira expresses the policy shown in the new instructions. Duke of Connaught will marry Princess Helena on Thursday. Parliament will debate national defense on Wednesday, so naval representatives will not continue the talks before Friday. (November 26, Reuters Electric)

[London] The US Chief Representative to the Naval Talks, Davis, met with the Japanese Ambassador to Britain, Matsudaira, this morning for an hour. According to the recent declaration by Yamamoto, the Japanese Chief Specialist Commissioner of the Navy, the naval issue has now reached the stage of discussing specific aspects. However, this morning's US-Japan talks did not seem to confirm Yamamoto's declaration. At the beginning of the talks, Ambassador Matsudaira first stated to Davis that the Japanese representative had not intended to acknowledge the British Navy's superiority to establish an agreement, and had not made such a proposal to Britain. In other words, Matsudaira has denied the outside world's rumors that Japan is preparing to establish a naval treaty based on the ratio of 5 for Britain, 4 for the United States, and 4 for Japan. However, since the strictness of Japan's proposed claims has been fully understood, the comfort that Matsudaira gave Davis in this morning's meeting was just diplomatic rhetoric. Therefore, the talks tonight were not limited to this point. Matsudaira also tried to convince Davis that Japan had not made a detailed reply to Britain's reconciliation plan, especially to the clause in the British proposal that certain provisions of the Washington Treaty should be retained after its abolition. Japan did not make a detailed reply to this statement, which probably refers to Article 19 of the Washington Treaty regarding the non-addition of defensive works in the Pacific. In short, Matsudaira has at least assured Davis from a procedural point of view that the door to negotiations is still open. The second part of the talks was about the outlook for the future after the abolition of the Washington Treaty, since the abolition of the Washington Treaty is a foregone conclusion. However, it seems that neither the Japanese nor the American representatives have reached any conclusions on this level. (November 26, Havas Electric)

Araki's Wild Rant 29

[Tokyo] Former Minister of the Army Sadao Araki gave a radio address on the 26th entitled "The Naval Disarmament Conference and the Standpoint of the Japanese Empire," using his qualifications as an army general to discuss naval issues, clarify the unity of army and navy defense, and promote national awareness of national defense. He briefly stated that even if Japan is in an isolated position, it must be willing to deal with national difficulties. (November 26, Japanese United Electric)

The Naval Conference is Gradually Becoming More Complex 30

Both Political and Substantive Issues are Raised

[London] The London Naval Preparatory Conference has been going on for a month, and the time for Japan to notify the abolition of the Washington Treaty is gradually approaching. It has now reached the crossroads of success or failure. The private meeting between Matsudaira and Davis held this week was the first private meeting between Japan and the United States. Because the negotiations are at a major turning point, they have become the focus of attention from all parties. The US attitude remains tough, clearly distinguishing between equality of naval power and equality of national defense security. Because of the fear that Japan's acquisition of equality of naval power will undermine the sense of national defense security, it resolutely maintains the current naval ratio system. Therefore, it is not permissible to be optimistic about the outcome of the US-Japan private meeting. At present, there are only three ways to break the situation, namely: (1) Gradually increase the Japanese ratio within a certain period to achieve equality; (2) Gradually reduce the naval power of Britain and the United States to achieve equality at a lower level than the current level; (3) Start discussing the issue of qualitative restrictions. Regarding the above three methods, Representative Yamamoto's compromise proposal is highly anticipated and hoped for. The agenda guiding the talks this week will likely not go beyond the scope of the deadline for achieving equality and the issue of qualitative restrictions. Since the beginning, the preparatory conference has gradually changed from a one-dimensional negotiation centered on the issue of heavy restrictions to a complex, multi-dimensional situation involving qualitative and political issues. (November 23, Japanese United Electric)

Japan No Longer Opposes Discussing Political Issues 31

Still Says the Manchuria Issue Should be Excluded

[Tokyo] There is a trend towards introducing political issues into the London Preparatory Conference. However, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently stated that it has not yet received any specific expressions from Britain and the United States regarding this matter. At a time when Japan's attitude is firm and unwavering, this proves that Britain and the United States lack confidence. When the Japanese government agreed to participate in the preparatory conference, the fact that East Asian political issues would not be introduced had been confirmed by Britain and the United States. It is unbelievable that Britain and the United States would propose discussions at this time. However, although the Japanese government opposes discussing the China issue and the Manchuria issue, it also expresses its support for discussing political issues that can establish the principle of peace and non-war between Britain, the United States, and Japan, and achieve the goal of maintaining world peace, so that naval negotiations can be successfully concluded. In addition, the Japanese government is convinced that Japan's disarmament plan is fair and appropriate, so the Japanese side has no intention of raising this type of political issue. (November 26, Dentsu Electric)

[Tokyo] The theory of establishing a new treaty at the Guandong Naval Preparatory Conference is gradually gaining traction. Countries are considering this issue with the expansion and strengthening of the Four-Power Treaty as the center. Therefore, there is currently a proposal to extend the validity period of the Four-Power Treaty by ten years in order to realize the new treaty. The procedure for extending the validity period of the Four-Power Treaty is not complicated and is easily agreed upon by various countries. Japan has no objection to the issue of extension. (November 26, Japanese United Electric)

If a War Occurs in Europe and Asia, Soviet Russia Will Be in a Pivotal Position 32

The United States is Now Eager to Resolve the Loan Negotiations

To Strengthen Soviet Russia's Military and Economic Power

French-Russian Negotiations Are Also Being Intensified

[Washington] People in Europe and the United States now regard Soviet Russia as the backbone in the event of a war in Europe and Asia. The US government wants to quickly resolve the loan negotiations with Russia to increase Soviet Russia's military and economic strength. Responsible parties believe that since Japan is determined to abolish the naval treaty, the Nine-Power Pact and the Four-Power Treaty will be torn up. The navy and diplomacy are thinking about ways to guarantee peace. The government's current focus is on maintaining the political status quo to await the clarification of the world's economic situation and naval issues. Although officials here deny that the issue of the status of Soviet Russia was considered during the current negotiations, fair responsible authorities believe that this is an inevitable result. (November 25, National Electric)

Roosevelt's New Deal is Trending Towards Liberalism 36

Cooperation Between the Government and the Financial Industry

Striving to Save the Economic Panic

The Debt Raising Method is Quite Clever

[Washington] According to the situation here today, President Roosevelt has trended towards liberalism. Observers, because business leaders wanted to know what the President's attitude was, said that judging from the President's measures in recent months, it can be seen that the "New Deal" has trended towards moderation. The impetus for radical change has been shifted by the conservative trend. The most radical action by the government at present is the attack on public utilities, such as the investigation of American Telephone and Telegraph Company. Although the company's employees said that they had no secrets and therefore welcomed the investigation, Wall Street believed that this was a hostile action by the government, because the result may lead to a reduction in the general public utility fees. As for the President's current conservative moves, there are about the following items:

(1) The government's way of changing the value of the dollar will no longer change; (2) Encourage bankers and business leaders to participate in the government's revival movement; (3) Oppose the silver act again.

The connection between the government and large merchants is also regarded as the most important development in Washington in recent months. Bankers, industrialists, and financiers have all expressed their cooperation with the President. For several weeks, the President has been listening to the various suggestions of the large industrialists, preparing to fight the economic panic again. Some observers believe that the large merchants' entry and exit of the White House is a sign of the temporary loss of power of the "brain trust," but those who are friendly to the government laugh it off. (November 25, National News Agency)

[New York] According to statistics compiled and released today by government securities expert Devin Company, the US government's method of raising debt under President Roosevelt's administration is more intelligent than any previous administration. The report stated that the current average interest rate on public debt is 3.02 percent, while the average interest rate on March 1 last year was 3.34 percent. Since March 1 last year, although the total amount of public debt has increased by 29 percent, the total amount of interest has only increased by 14.7 percent. (November 25, National News Agency)

[Tokyo] Governor of the Bank of Japan, Hijikata, made the following remarks regarding the impact of Finance Minister Fujii's resignation due to illness on financial circles:

Finance Minister Fujii's sudden resignation due to illness is quite astonishing. However, the fixed financial policy of the current cabinet is unlikely to change abruptly as a result. Moreover, the budget for the next fiscal year has already been finalized and was established yesterday. Therefore, financial circles are unlikely to be affected. Stock trading on the 26th also did not experience any significant fluctuations. However, I sincerely sympathize with the Finance Minister for resigning midway through his term due to illness. Yutian is in Utter Chaos 93

The Pseudo-Army Occupies Important Towns and Villages

Tianjin Correspondence: Among the counties in the war zone, Yutian is the most chaotic recently. The number of bandits is almost uncountable. Almost every village and town in the county has bandits, and there is almost no village where robbery does not occur every day. The strength of the local militia is only enough to defend the outskirts of the county and block large groups of bandits from entering, but the bandits lurking within the territory are like rats gnawing and insects eating away from the inside, and there is no power to suppress them. The former County Magistrate, Chen Baosheng, was transferred to the province due to the Gong Yue case, awaiting another appointment. The newly appointed County Magistrate, Huang Zhongkai, although he has taken office, is controlled by the Security Reinforcement Team, and government orders are not implemented. He only flatters the Security Team to protect himself. Recently, the areas occupied by bandits include Fengwu Town, bordering Fengrun and Yutian, with about six or seven hundred people. They actually control the post and telecommunications, block traffic, and issue orders to nearby villages. Lin Cangnan Town is also occupied by more than a hundred bandits, who go out dozens of miles during the day to rob villages. These bandits all avoid calling themselves bandits, claiming to be a certain detachment or brigade of the Pseudo-East Asia Alliance Army of Shi Yousan and Liu Guitang, or a certain regiment headquarters, brigade headquarters, or detachment headquarters. The people of Yutian are deaf and blind because the traffic is controlled by bandits, and they cannot distinguish the authenticity of these bandit troops. Those who have the strength to escape move elsewhere, and those who do not have the strength to move far away are left to be slaughtered by the bandits. Although the authorities are well aware of the situation here, they cannot send troops to suppress them due to the limitations of the war zone, and the situation is also extremely complicated, which cannot be resolved by simple military action. (22nd)

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today's listed price is 139 shillings and 6 pence, 1 pence higher than Saturday.

London Silver: The silver market was stable today. Speculators bought in the morning, and there were not many suppliers. The spot price is 24.5 pence, and the futures price is 24.625 pence, both up 0.0625.

Exchange Rate

After the authorities initially used the stabilization fund to adjust the exchange market, there were fewer and fewer transactions. The pound sterling showed a weak trend against gold coins and against the US dollar. The opening price of the US exchange rate was 4 US dollars and 99 cents, 1.25 lower than the closing exchange rate between the US and the UK on Saturday. It continued to decline slightly in the morning, but the number was very small. Prospects for the Japanese Extraordinary Diet 95

The Two Parties, Seiyukai and Minseito, will Fight Together

Budget Compilation Repeatedly Frustrated

In a constitutional political country, special attention is naturally paid to the parliament, because the parliament is the representative body of public opinion, urging the government to do all kinds of work required by the people. The recent parliament in Japan is still the sole legislative body, but in fact, most of the public does not seem to be very enthusiastic about it. Even political parties that specialize in political life do not have any performance that is sufficient to represent the public. On the contrary, the public is very indifferent to political parties, and seems to feel that the relationship is not close and does not hope that they can solve their problems in the parliament. The depression of political parties is an undeniable fact.

The Minseito is the party of the current government, but since the establishment of the Okada cabinet, except for the fact that its foreign policy has followed the previous policy without change and has not been criticized by the public, the rest has been unremarkable, and general public opinion has little favor. Therefore, although the Minseito is considered to be consistent with the government and should theoretically support the government's proposals, the Okada cabinet's lukewarm attitude towards the increase in taxes has aroused a lot of resentment. Even the discontented voices within the Minseito can be heard everywhere. The most obvious symbol is the joint movement of the Seiyukai and Minseito.

The work of cooperation between the Seiyukai and Minseito did not start today. Since the May 15th assassination of Inukai and the shake-up of parliamentary politics, every political season, someone has loudly advocated the movement for cooperation between political parties or a one-party system for the whole country, but none of them have had any effect. What's more, the Seiyukai has almost 300 members in the parliament, accounting for an absolute majority of the 466 seats in the House of Representatives. Even if the Minseito is added, it may not be useful.

The reason why this time the movement for cooperation between the two parties is relatively strong is, firstly, it is affected by the reform of the organization of institutions in "Manchuria", and secondly, it is stimulated by the booklet "The Essence of National Defense" issued by the military. Because the institutions in "Manchuria" were originally co-governed by civilian and military officials. In other words, they are capitalists and quite powerful managers. However, in recent years, they have not been very at ease with their investment in "Manchuria", and some people are even unwilling to invest new capital anymore, fearing that they will not be able to control it in the future and that safety is not sufficient. But after all, there is room for development there, and excess capital should be invested. However, they have long felt that it is inappropriate to transfer all political power to the military as it is now. The issue of the booklet issued by the military caused considerable resentment in the House of Peers and the House of Representatives, but they dared not express it because they were afraid of the power of the military. If the Seiyukai and Minseito can really unite, it may be easier to deal with. Moreover, since Wakatsuki Reijiro resigned as president of the Minseito, there is no one to head the party for a while, and the cooperation movement naturally feels necessary. Suzuki Kisaburo of the Seiyukai is not very enthusiastic about the union of the two parties, but on the one hand, there is Kusuhara Fusanosuke's "one-party system for the whole country," and on the other hand, there is Yamamoto Jotaro's "theory of supporting constitutional politics," and after Tokonami's entry into the cabinet, problems have arisen in the party's control, so Suzuki cannot but accommodate the proposal for the union of the Seiyukai and Minseito. However, it is doubtful whether the union can reach what extent, whether it can fight against the current government with a unified party, because supporting the constitution is, after all, an abstract and empty statement and cannot raise the spirit of union. Unless a general attack is launched on the Okada cabinet and the union is formed in the movement to overthrow the cabinet, it is only possible. Suzuki, as the leader of a purely opposition party, certainly supports this move, and the Kusuhara faction also generally agrees, but he intends to support Ugaki Kazushige as the president of the party or support General Minami Jiro as the prime minister of the cabinet. Yamamoto (Jotaro) does not seem to be very much in favor of actively overthrowing the cabinet. Although the Minseito also tends to the movement to overthrow the cabinet, it is not determined to immediately call on the cabinet members from the party to withdraw from the cabinet, but is only going around in circles on the issue of reform. In this case, the union movement will not only fail to unite on practical issues, but there is also a risk of separation.

The strength of the current cabinet itself was originally composed of the military, the bureaucracy, and political parties, and it is fundamentally difficult to be consistent. We see the disputes over the issue of the increased budget. The military's position naturally overrides everything. Although it has repeatedly made concessions now, the result is probably that military spending will account for 46% to 50% of the total national treasury expenditure. Other expenses, such as disaster relief, have also increased considerably, but compared with national defense spending, they are ultimately a minority. In fact, Finance Minister Fujii, who is close to financiers and industrial capital, cannot but take into account the current financial situation and cannot disobey the demands of the military. The result is that it is probably not the parliament that will overthrow the cabinet, but the contradictions contained within the cabinet itself. (November 22, 1934, Tokyo)

Japanese Urgently Seek to Develop Gold Mines in Jehol 96

Ten Major Gold Mountains Discovered in the Yinshan Mountains

The Most Extensive Coal Seams in the Congling Mountains

Chengde Correspondence: Jehol is mountainous, so it is rich in mineral resources. Along the Shanhaiguan border wall, far from Kaiping and Luanzhou in Hebei, between Shimenzhai Chaoyang Xinqiu, belonging to the Congling Mountains, there are extensive coal seams. From the Harqin to the Ongniut Banner and the Han tribes, belonging to the Yinshan Mountains, the Japanese have recently discovered "Ten Major Gold Mountains." The Japanese are now investigating and studying and planning to mine. The location and content of the gold mines are listed below for reference.

(1) Xindaba Gold Mountain, located in Xinqiu Nanli Yu, is embedded in granite. There are two gold-bearing quartz veins, one is 350 feet long and 1.5 to 5 feet wide, and the other is also 350 feet long and 2 to 3.5 feet wide, both containing gold at a rate of 2 to 8 parts per million and silver at a rate of 8 to 10 percent. (2) Xu Jiabei Man Gold Mountain, located 1.5 miles south of the Beizi Mansion in Beigushan, Chaoyang, has two quartz veins penetrating gneiss, one extending 500 meters and 2 inches to 1.3 feet wide, and the other extending 600 meters and 2 inches to 7 inches wide, which increases to 3 feet at the outcrop in the old pit. If the trace of the road to gold is obtained from the first two veins, the extension of the vein is very promising. (3) Shang Shelihu Gold Mountain, located 3 miles south of the Beizi Mansion in Gushan, has Baigu Matai Stone penetrating gneiss, with two quartz veins, one extending 500 meters and 1 to 4.5 feet wide, and the other extending 300 meters and the width is unknown, reportedly 4 to 5 feet. The gold content of the two veins is 3 parts per 100,000. The pit is currently full of water, so it has been suspended. There is great hope if a drainage machine is used. (4) Yangjiawanzi Gold Mountain, located 150 miles northeast of Jianping, has four quartz veins of Baigu Matai Stone penetrating gneiss, one 1,000 feet long and 1 to 4.5 feet wide, the second 800 feet long and 4.5 feet wide, the third 1,500 feet long and 1 to 3 feet wide, and the fourth 1,100 feet long and 5 inches wide. The gold content of the four veins is 3 to 6 parts per million, which is the most promising gold vein in Jehol. (5) Jinchanggouliang Gold Mountain, located 16 miles northwest of Chaoyang, has ten gold-bearing quartz veins embedded in gneiss, the largest being 700 meters long and 2 inches to 1 foot wide, containing gold at a rate of 2 to 8 parts per 100,000, but the vein is small, which is its shortcoming. (6) Lai Maozi Gold Mountain, located 1.5 miles east of Jinchanggouliang, has gold-bearing quartz veins embedded in coal and rock, with a number of veins ranging from one to five, the largest being 1,300 meters long and 1 inch to 7 feet wide, containing gold at a rate of 1 part per 10,000 to 2 parts per 100,000. (7) Xiao Changquan Gold Mountain, located 100 miles southeast of Jianping, has four quartz veins embedded in gneiss, the longest being 1,500 feet and the other five or six hundred feet, with a vein about one foot wide containing 2 to 8 parts per million. It is very promising if a drainage machine is installed. (8) Jiguan Mountain, located northeast of Chifeng Nan Harachili Prefecture, is filled in the gaps between Gang Stone or Hua Yan Banshi, mainly with quartz veins, containing gold at a rate of 2 to 10 parts per 100,000. (9) Nianzigou Gold Mountain, located 30 miles northwest of Chengde, has a simple quartz vein deposit of cloud stone, with three veins containing gold at a rate of 2 parts per 100,000, starting from 5 feet wide. (10) Luotuo Gou Gold Mountain, located about 25 miles northwest of Chengde, has a long-grown bed and is very promising. After checking that Jehol has been seized by the Japanese, the great mountains are no longer ours. I wonder what our people will think after hearing the news that the Japanese are mining gold in Jehol.

Members of the Mongolian Political Council Will Go South to Visit Chiang Kai-shek 97

The compatriots in Beiping were previously panicked due to the disappearance of Han Fenglin, but in view of the difficult times for the country, they did not dare to make any expressions other than waiting for the government to investigate the matter thoroughly. Taking advantage of Bu Ying Dalai's visit to Nanjing, the compatriots in Beiping specially appointed Bu Ying Dalai as the representative of the compatriots and attached a statement when meeting Chairman Chiang, so that the whereabouts of Han Fenglin would be revealed as soon as possible to dispel doubts, etc. (24th)

The Success of the Fifth Encirclement Campaign: Huichang is Completely Recovered 98

There are No More Bandit Areas in Jiangxi Province

Scattered Bandits in the Four Townships are Awaiting Suppression

Nanchang Correspondence: Huichang is the gateway for southeastern Jiangxi to Fujian and Guangdong, bordering Ruijin to the north, Xunwu to the south, Yudu and Anyuan to the west, and Wuping in Fujian and Pingyuan in Guangdong to the east. It is also the key point of the bandit areas of the three provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi. The throat of Huichang connecting Fujian and Guangdong is at Yunmenling. Before sea transportation was available, it was the hub for trade in the border areas of the three provinces. There was a customs office, and the terrain was dangerous, making it a must for military competition. In the past, the Red Army's strategy was to defend against Guangdong and attack Jiangxi and Fujian, that is, to defend Guangdong with Huichang Yunmenling and consolidate the rear of its pseudo-central government. Ye Jianying led the troops directly under the pseudo-central government, such as students from the Red Army School, the Pseudo-Guard Division, the First Supplementary Division, and Chen Yi and other forces in the Pseudo-Jiangxi Provincial Military Region, and deployed them in the Yunmenling area, building solid fortifications to defend to the death. The Zhu-Mao pseudo-1st, 3rd, 5th, 7th, 8th, 9th, 10th, and 12th pseudo-army groups were able to harass eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian with peace of mind, which shows the importance of its relationship. The Fifth Encirclement Campaign by the National Army used the Southern Route Army to attack Yunmen, directly attacking the heart of the pseudo-central government to destroy the bandits. If Huichang could have been captured earlier, the encirclement campaign could have ended earlier. However, when the Northern Route Army captured Shicheng and the Eastern Route Army captured Tingzhou, and the Red Army fled west with all its strength, the Southern Route Army was unable to advance on Huichang according to the planned plan due to fierce battles in Xinfeng, Dayu, and Nankang. The plan was changed, and the Eastern Route Army took Ruijin Huichang from east to west. According to publicly released news, after Li Yutang, Liu Kan and other troops advanced towards Huichang from Wuping and Shanghang, the pseudo-independent regiments, local guerrillas, and scattered bandits along the way were all defeated. On the 20th, they surrounded Huichang County. Seeing that the situation was not good, the remnant bandits abandoned the city and fled west. The Li Division then entered the county seat on the 23rd to handle the aftermath. Since 1927, Jiangxi has been shrouded in Red Terror. More than 20 of the 81 counties in the province (now Guangze in Fujian and Wuyuan in Anhui have been划赣共八十三 counties) were completely occupied by bandits. More than 20 counties guarded by the National Army existed in name only. More than 20 counties where bandits appeared and disappeared irregularly were trapped in the situation where bandits went when the army came and bandits came when the army left. The truly safe areas were only Nanchang, Xinjian, Jiujiang, Jinkou, and five or six other counties. As of the 17th of this month, under the gradual advancement of the National Army's steady encirclement and blockade, only Huichang County remained in the hands of bandits in all counties in the province. Now that Huichang has also been recovered, there are no longer any bandits occupying towns in Jiangxi. Only the scattered bandits in the newly recovered areas and the heavily bandit areas in the four townships urgently need to be suppressed and appeased. (November 24)

Salt Affairs Bureau Sends Personnel to Inspect Salt Affairs in Shaanxi Province 99

Li Yujie Arrives in the Province, First Inspecting Guanzhong

Xi'an Correspondence: In order to coordinate and rectify salt affairs in various localities and increase salt tax revenue, the Ministry of Finance has dispatched commissioners to various provinces for inspection, in order to facilitate rectification. Li Yujie, the Shaanxi Province Salt Affairs Inspection Commissioner, arrived in the province some days ago and is staying at the Shaanxi Provincial Ministry of Finance Salt Affairs Revenue Bureau. According to Li, the Ministry of Finance, in view of the fact that since the second year of the Republic of China, when Yuan Shikai privately borrowed 20 million gold pounds from the Five-Nation Banking Consortium, using the national salt tax as collateral, all subsequent salt affairs in China have been subject to foreign supervision, resulting in the outflow of rights and interests and numerous loopholes, which has greatly harmed the national treasury and economy. Therefore, in October of last year, the Ministry of Finance established the Salt Affairs Inspection General Office, with branch offices established in various production areas and salt tax revenue bureaus established in sales areas, specializing in salt affairs and tax revenue matters, under the unified jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance, in order to prevent foreigners from profiting from it. However, since the salt tax in various localities was placed under the management of the Ministry of Finance last year, active efforts have been made to rectify it. Now, in order to increase tax revenue, commissioners have been dispatched to various provinces for inspection. The revenue from salt tax in this province, in addition to the regular expenses of the tax bureau and the payment of foreign debt installments, has been approved by the Ministry of Finance to be allocated to the province's entire education fund, in order to expand education and cultivate talents. This time, I came to Shaanxi, have already met with Chairman Shao, and plan to contact various party and government organs in the coming days. I plan to inspect the inland area of Guanzhong first, and then proceed to the Hanzhong and Yulin areas. If there is an opportunity, I also plan to visit Lanzhou. (23rd)

Songjiang 100

Water Police Captain Captures Thief in Fengjing

Hu Tu, the captain of the Water Police Team stationed in Songjiang of the Provincial Public Security Team, recently received a secret report that the bandit Gu A'bu was recently discovered in Fengjing. It is said that the criminal is from outside the North Gate of this county, 30 years old. He used to work in a certain restaurant in Fengjing. Later, because of his association with bad friends and his bad behavior, the owner, fearing that he would take excessive action, dismissed Gu. Since Gu lost his job, his life became more difficult, so he associated with bandits and committed crimes in the Fengjing area. After the government investigated, the criminal disappeared without a trace. Now, a informant saw him and reported to the team, so he was captured without resistance.

Extensive Establishment of Warehouses to Relieve Rural Areas

The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously ordered all counties to extensively establish warehouses in order to relieve rural areas. After receiving the order, this county consulted with the Farmers Bank and convened local gentry to discuss preparations. It has been decided to set up locations in Tinglin, Sijing, and Huayang Bridge. The Farmers Bank will also follow the case and set up two agricultural product warehouses in Cangqiao and other places. The methods are roughly the same. All agricultural products and agricultural tools can be used to apply for loans from the warehouse. Approximately 70% of the value of 100 yuan can be pledged, with a monthly interest rate of 9%, and a warehouse rental fee of 6%. It can be redeemed at any time, so that the farmers' economy can be used for turnover.

Disputes over the Exchange Rate of Rice and Bean Businesses

In the spring of this year, the rice and bean businesses in this county decided to change the 99 exchange rate to 98.4 because the price of grain was low and it was difficult to maintain expenses. This caused opposition from the grain merchants in Bengbu, who sent personnel to Wuxi to negotiate. The county chamber of commerce in this county invited grain merchants from Wuxi, Wujin, and Bengbu to discuss a solution. As a result, it was decided that when the price of yellow beans is below five yuan per stone, the 99 exchange rate will be changed to 98.6. If it rises to five yuan or more, the 99 exchange rate will be restored. All three parties agreed, and the dispute was resolved. Recently, the Bengbu Grain Industry Association, the Transportation Association, the Grain Merchants Association, etc., stated that the current price of yellow beans has risen to more than five yuan, but Wuxi has not yet restored the 99 exchange rate. Therefore, they specially requested the county chamber of commerce in that city to send a telegram to the county chamber of commerce in this county yesterday, asking it to immediately stop the 98.6 exchange rate and restore the 99 exchange rate, so as to avoid further disputes.

Jiaxing 105

Robbery and Injury Occurs in Wangdian Countryside

In Zhangjiaqiao, Guojie Township, Wangdian, Jiaxing, the home of Jin Zhou, a farmer, was entered by several bandits speaking the local dialect and the dialect of traveling merchants at about 1 a.m. on the 25th. They broke in by digging a hole in the wall and held long spears and sharp knives. They shouted to forbid any noise and tied up Jin Zhou, Jin Youguan, Jin Xiaoguan, and worker Yao A'da with ropes. The bandits then broke into the inner room and searched at will. They poured kerosene on Jin Zhou and set her on fire, forcing her to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Jin Youguan's chest and face were injured by gunfire, and Jin Xiaoguan and Yao A'da's heads were injured. Jin Zhou said that there was no hidden silver in the house, so even though she was burned by the fire, she could not tell them. The bandits also searched the house, but did not find any cash. When dawn was approaching, the bandits took away clothes, soft goods, and silver dollars worth more than 300 yuan. Afterwards, a report was made to the Fifth District Office and the Fifth Public Security Bureau, who sent personnel to investigate. On the 26th, the injured people were taken to the local branch court to be examined, and a request was made to order the arrest of the stolen goods and bandits.

As a result, the New Life Bookstore, Shunfeng Clothing Store, a certain cigarette shop, Yi Ji Lu Photo Studio, and Jiujiang Lou Restaurant were burned, causing significant losses.

Anhui Province Loan Agreement Negotiated, Draft Contract Signed 108

To Be Officially Signed in Wuhu After Provincial Government Approval

Totaling 1.2 Million, to Be Disbursed in Three Installments and Repaid in 20 Months

The Anhui Provincial Government, due to the extraordinary severity of this year's drought and the sharp decline in tax revenue, felt that administrative expenses were difficult to manage. It therefore contacted the Central and five other banks to negotiate a loan of 1.2 million yuan to cope with the situation. The loan has been fully negotiated since Mao Longzhang, the Director of the Anhui Provincial Department of Finance, came to Shanghai to negotiate. A draft contract was signed last Saturday (the 24th), and Director Mao took it back to Anhui yesterday afternoon to report. After it is approved by the Provincial Government, it will be officially signed in Wuhu with the branches of the borrowing banks. The details of the situation learned by the New News Agency reporter are as follows:

Negotiation Process

The Anhui Provincial Government had previously obtained approval from the Central Government to issue 900,000 yuan of local treasury bonds for the 23rd year of the Republic. For the sake of procedural convenience, the issuance of the treasury bonds was suspended, and Director of Finance Mao Longzhang came to Shanghai to borrow 800,000 yuan from the Central and five other banks within the approved quota for treasury bonds. Together with the 400,000 yuan loan previously negotiated with the five banks to make up for the province's budget deficit, the total amount was 1.2 million yuan to be used for administrative expenses. The entire salt surplus allocated by the Ministry of Finance to the province was used as a guarantee fund. After Director Mao came to Shanghai, he repeatedly negotiated with the borrowing banks, and a full agreement was only reached last Saturday. The loan draft contract was signed.

Signing the Contract

After the loan was negotiated, Director Mao invited representatives from the borrowing banks to the Central Bank on the third floor at 3 p.m. last Saturday to make a final decision. After revising the draft contract clause by clause, the representatives of the banks signed the draft contract. The representatives who signed were Zhou Bangxin, the Deputy Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Central Bank, Cheng Muhao, the Deputy Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China, Zhang Peishen, the Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of Communications, Liu Huizhi, the General Manager of the China Industrial Bank, Zou Bingwen, the Deputy Manager of the Head Office of the Shanghai Bank, and Mao Longzhang, the Director of the Anhui Department of Finance. It is also understood that the five banks mailed the draft contract to their Wuhu branches yesterday. After it is approved by the Anhui Provincial Government, it will be officially signed.

Five Banks Undertake the Loan

The banks that undertook the loan include the Central, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, and China Industrial Bank. The total amount of the loan is 1.2 million yuan. The Central Bank will undertake 600,000 yuan, and the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, and China Industrial Bank will undertake 600,000 yuan separately, for a total of 1.2 million yuan. The guarantee for the loan is the same as the guarantee for the Anhui Province local treasury bonds approved for issuance by the Central Government, that is, the entire salt surplus allocated by the Ministry of Finance to the province, with an annual interest rate of 9.6%, or a monthly interest rate of 8%.

Disbursing in Installments

The method of disbursing the funds is also stipulated in the contract. It will be disbursed in three installments. The first installment of 800,000 yuan will be disbursed on December 1 of this year, the second installment of 200,000 yuan will be disbursed on February 1 next year (end of the lunar year), and the third installment of 200,000 yuan will be disbursed on June 1 next year (lunar Dragon Boat Festival). It has also been decided that repayment will begin in February next year, and the full amount will be repaid in 20 months.

Mao Returns to Anhui

Mao Longzhang, the Director of the Anhui Department of Finance, has now completed his official business in Shanghai and left Shanghai for Anhui at 4 p.m. yesterday with the signed draft contract to report the progress to Liu Zhenhua, the Chairman of Anhui Province. Once it is approved by the Provincial Government, it will be officially signed with the Wuhu branches of the Central and other banks.

Finance Minister Kong Discusses Ministry of Finance's Wholesale of Cigarette Stamp Tax 109

The Purpose Is to Allocate Funds for Regular National Treasury Expenditures

Construction Bank and Other Companies Undertake the Purchase at 92% of Face Value

The Explanation of Mortgage Loans Is a Misunderstanding

Shen Shi News Agency reports that in order to supplement national treasury expenditures, the Ministry of Finance recently wholesaled 30 million yuan of newly issued cigarette stamp tax tickets to the China Construction Bank and various banks in this port, to be paid in twelve installments. The Shen Shi News Agency reporter visited Kong last night and was informed of the purpose of the funds and the negotiation process. The details are as follows:

Finance Minister Kong Speaks

According to Kong, it has recently been rumored that the Ministry of Finance mortgaged 30 million yuan of cigarette stamp tax to the Shanghai banking community. This is indeed a fact, but it is not a "mortgage." It is that the Ministry of Finance has approved the wholesale of all 30 million yuan of newly issued cigarette stamp tax tickets to the China Construction Bank, which will then promote and undertake the purchase to its shareholder banks. The Ministry of Finance and the Construction Bank have now fully negotiated, and the Construction Bank is directly responsible to the Ministry of Finance for paying the cash.

Use of the Huge Sum

As for the Ministry of Finance, the cash will still be used to supplement regular national treasury expenditures and has no special purpose. Therefore, the wholesale of 30 million cigarette stamps is just the Ministry of Finance hoping to obtain cash for application in advance and is not in the nature of a loan. The Construction Bank itself has decided to undertake one-third of the total purchase, amounting to 10 million yuan. The remaining 20 million yuan will be allocated to the shareholder banks of the Construction Bank for undertaking the purchase. This is an internal matter of the company and is not the Ministry of Finance mortgaging loans to banks.

Payment at 92% of Face Value

Kong continued that the Ministry of Finance would allow a payment of 92% of face value for the wholesale, with 8% as the profit of the undertakers. Yesterday's report of 93% was inaccurate. It is stipulated that payment will be made in twelve installments, that is, starting next month, the silver company will be responsible for paying the Ministry of Finance each month, with a limit of one year for payment. The Ministry of Finance will then deliver 3 million yuan of cigarette stamp tax tickets to the Central Bank each month. After the Central Bank sells the tax tickets, the resulting cash will be paid to the undertakers in installments.

Two Telegrams from the All-Zhejiang Public Association to the Zhejiang Provincial Government 110

Appealing for the Disaster Victims in Zhejiang Province

Re-survey the Disaster Areas, Respectfully Addressed to Chairman Lu of the Zhejiang Provincial Government: The drought disaster in Zhejiang Province this year has been extremely severe. We are currently in the rainy season, and while we urgently hope for rain, the planting of farmland is incomplete. Those that have been planted have just been transplanted, and their roots are fragile and unable to withstand the scorching sun. They have all been baked to death. According to statistics, the harvest in various counties throughout the province is only 30% to 40%. Those near the water have some harvest, but they have exhausted dozens of days and nights to pump water for irrigation, and the income is not worth the effort. They are also equally pitiful. We have heard that the Provincial Committee has investigated and reported the disaster situation and harvest quantity in various counties, such as Jiaxing County being set at 65%, Wuxing County at 50%, and Deqing County at 45%. These reports are inaccurate and inconsistent with the disaster situation in various regions. The Provincial Committee and others came to the border for investigation after the autumn harvest, and the disaster situation had already passed. Moreover, they did not conduct surveys acre by acre, but only relied on the narratives of village elders and neighborhood chiefs and made arbitrary conclusions, which are not enough to satisfy the people. This drought has lasted for more than three months, which is rare in the past century. The withered stems and leaves sway in the scorching sun, and there is no harvest, which is shocking. After successive years of famine, at a time when the countryside is collapsing, it is already difficult for middle-class farmers to survive, let alone the poor. Taxes are the sacred duty of the people, but in the midst of this disaster relief, it seems that we should be lenient so that the disaster victims can avoid being compensated. The investigation of disaster-stricken fields should be based on facts, and it is better to be lenient than harsh. It is hoped that harsh policies will be eliminated and that the benefits of tax reduction will be extended. Our Association has compassion for our hometown and cannot remain indifferent. For this reason, we urgently request that your Excellency approve the dispatch of personnel to re-survey the counties most severely affected by the disaster and grant them full exemption. Those that are slightly less severe should be reduced based on verification. All past arrears should be postponed to relieve the people's suffering and prioritize disaster relief. We respectfully bow nine times on behalf of the disaster victims. Shanghai All-Zhejiang Public Association.

Organize Work Relief, Respectfully Addressed to Chairman Lu of the Zhejiang Provincial Government: This year's drought in Zhejiang has caused a disaster. The severity of the disaster and the tragedy of the situation have been reported by various counties and are already well known. There is no need to reiterate them. We have now heard that the Provincial Relief Committee has negotiated and obtained approval from your Excellency to allocate 1 million yuan in cash from the newly issued public bonds. Various charitable organizations in Shanghai, such as the Chinese Jisenghui, the China Foreign Relief Association, and the Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association, have also raised funds to assist in the joint implementation of winter relief. However, the disaster area is too wide, and the counties have identified nearly 3 million disaster victims who cannot survive without relief. Although the investigators have conducted house-to-house surveys and strictly eliminated some, it is still felt that the disaster is severe and the funds are insufficient to distribute. Since all are disaster victims, it is not only impossible to have one area receive relief while another is denied, but it is also unbearable. We propose to quickly convert the 6 million yuan of public bonds designated for work relief into cash and implement it simultaneously with winter relief. This will allow the strong to live by working and focus on distributing winter relief to the elderly, weak, women, and children. The number of recipients can be greatly reduced, and there will be no worry about insufficient relief funds. The future of the Zhejiang disaster is promising. Our Association appeals for the disaster victims in our hometown. For this reason, we urgently request that your Excellency quickly order the Department of Finance to raise funds to alleviate the disaster and eliminate the tragedy. We will be infinitely grateful. Shanghai All-Zhejiang Public Association.

Shanghai Money Market Extraordinarily Tight 112

Call Loan Rate Rose to 28 Cents Yesterday

The Demand for Silver Coins in Shanghai Is Therefore Increasing Daily

The daily call loan rate in the Ningbo Road Money Market has soared due to the extraordinarily tight money market, and the forward discount has also increased. The details are as follows:

Continued Soaring

The call loan rate in the Ningbo Road Money Market yesterday was 28 cents for the first session at 8:30 a.m. and 28 cents for the second session at 12:30 p.m. As for the forward discount, it opened at 43 cents yesterday afternoon (that is, a discount of 43 cents per 1,000 yuan). The call loan rate is usually only five or six cents, but it has now soared from five or six cents to 15 cents, 25 cents, and reached a peak of 28 cents.

Various Reasons

The New Sound News Agency reporter learned from the banking and money industry that the high call loan rate is due to the increasing demand for silver dollars in the city. The reasons are that agricultural products such as cotton and miscellaneous grains are being launched on the market one after another, and businesses are importing silver into the interior to purchase them. In addition, public bonds issued by various provinces are being mortgaged for loans from Shanghai banks, and silver is also being exported, resulting in a decrease in silver reserves in the city, which has led to this phenomenon.

Suzuki and Southwestern Figures Discuss Sino-Japanese Cooperation

Guo Wen News Agency reports that Japan's long-standing designs on South China are evidenced by the so-called "Across the Strait Conference" held in Taiwan and the purchase of military equipment by the Japanese on behalf of the Southwestern military and the employment of more than ten Japanese military officers in Guangxi, which stirred up student unrest. Its emphasis on South China is evident. Recently, Lieutenant General Suzuki, after inspecting Guangdong and Guangxi, convened resident army military attachés from various places in South and North China in Shanghai on the 17th and 18th of this month and held an important secret meeting at the Donghe Foreign Firm on Peng Road, Hongkou. There is now no anti-Japanese sentiment in Guangdong and Guangxi, and Japanese goods are selling well. They (referring to Hu, Chen, Li, and Bai) are convinced that Sino-Japanese friendship must start with economic cooperation. Therefore, I am convinced that Japan should pay full attention to this point in order to gradually promote the reality of friendly relations between China and Japan in the economic field and to consolidate the foundation of lasting peace in the Orient. After the meeting adjourned, the military attachés are now leaving Shanghai one after another. It is also heard that a certain military attaché has been appointed to return to Tokyo yesterday to report to the military. As for the content of the meeting, due to its confidential nature, the details are unknown. However, it is rumored that the result of the meeting suggested to the Japanese military that the situation in East China, South China, and North China is different, and the corresponding policies should therefore be different.

Petition to the Capital Fails, Ready to Close Down

A report from the Huadong News Agency states that in order to unify the postal system, the Ministry of Transportation has specially ordered the Directorate General of Posts to strictly order domestic private postal services to cease operations, and has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to issue a general order to all provincial, municipal, military, and police authorities to assist the post office in suppressing them, ensuring that they all close down within a set period. Petition to the Capital Ultimately Unsuccessful

Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Huadong News Agency inquired at the Quansheng Private Postal Service in Shanghai and learned that since the Ministry of Transportation ordered all private postal services nationwide to close down within this year, industry colleagues from private postal services across the country, fearing that their livelihoods would be cut off and their future would be difficult to sustain, have successively dispatched representatives to the capital to petition the central government. Preparing to Close Down Due to the Situation

Currently, November is almost over, and the deadline is approaching in an instant. There is only one month left until the end of the year. Industry colleagues in inland areas such as Hankou, Hangzhou, Changsha, Nanchang, Jinan, Xuzhou, Ningbo, Suzhou, Changzhou, Songjiang, Wenzhou, and Zhenjiang have already been urged by the local police bureau, at the request of the local post office, to close down by the end of the year. Private postal services in these areas have no room for maneuver, so they are all preparing to close down.

Four Bureaus Urge Closure Earnestly

There are a total of 54 private postal services in Shanghai. The Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, as well as the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Public Utilities Bureau, and Social Affairs Bureau, in accordance with the request of the Postal Administration and following the instructions of the Executive Yuan, dispatched detectives and staff yesterday morning to earnestly urge them to close down one by one within their respective jurisdictions. Now, due to the situation, the industry is preparing to close down by the end of the year.

Aftermath Problems Particularly Difficult

However, the aftermath problem after the closure of the private postal services is particularly difficult. Private postal services were founded in the early Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty and have a history of hundreds of years. They have been painstakingly managed and have worked hard to gain the trust of the people. No fewer than 100,000 people depend on this for a living. Therefore, there have been no surpluses in the past century of efforts to develop credit. Now that it has been decided to close down by the end of the year, 100,000 employees of private postal services nationwide will be completely unemployed, resulting in labor-management dismissal problems. The capital side has no surplus funds to provide severance pay, and the labor side will find it difficult to maintain their future livelihoods, so it is considered very serious.

Private Postal Service Guild Hall Held Another Meeting Yesterday

Yesterday afternoon, representatives of the national private postal service industry held an emergency representative meeting again at the Private Postal Service Guild Hall on Lixian'gua Street, starting from 4:00 PM and ending at 6:00 PM. More than 30 representatives, including Hua Yunjin, Yin Yuantong, Wang Tongwen, Ren Shiting, and Wu Yunyu, attended the meeting. Representatives were immediately elected to draft a memorial and decided to submit petitions to the municipal government, the municipal party headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Directorate General of Posts, and other related agencies this Wednesday or Thursday to explain the difficult situation. It is also understood that the representatives plan to go to Beijing in batches before the Fifth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang, first individually requesting each member of the Central Committee, and then gathering again on December 10 to petition the meeting.

Appropriate Jobs for Unemployed Employees

At present, although the government also recognizes that private postal services are disseminators of culture in China, the postal service is a state-run business in all countries around the world. The prevalence of private postal services fundamentally conflicts with the postal service, so it has no choice but to suppress them painfully. The aftermath of the livelihoods of unemployed employees is indeed a major problem. According to a semi-official source familiar with this industry, the government has made the utmost determination to urge private postal services to cease operations, but is hesitant about appropriate jobs for unemployed employees. In fact, the most appropriate placement method would be to send this large number of employees to border areas where post offices are scarce to establish post offices, because there are many hardworking and diligent people in the private postal service industry, and they also have a rough understanding of writing. If they can discuss this with each other, it will be beneficial to all aspects of China's cultural and transportation construction, and the livelihoods of more than 100,000 people can also be resolved.

He Yingqin and Others Go to the Capital 116

He Yingqin, Zhu Jiahua, Zeng Zhongming, Zou Lin, Zhou Xiangxian, Zeng Yangfu, Lu Chao, and others took the night express train to the capital yesterday.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Inspects Haiheng Vessel Yesterday 117

Shipowner Decides to Use Chinese Nationals

Absolutely Will Not Yield to Hong Kong

After the second new vessel, Haiheng, of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company arrived in Shanghai, it entered the No. 3 New Dock of the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Plant of the Naval Department in Gaochangmiao. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Zhao Yuntai, section chief of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Marine Department, and engineers from the Shanghai representative office of the British shipyard that built the vessel went to Gaochangmiao to inspect the machinery. After the inspection is completed, the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Plant will paint it. The company plans to take over on the 29th. However, regarding the issue of the shipmaster, the Hong Kong Marine Department insists that Chinese must take an exam, otherwise even the first mate must be filled by foreign personnel before a passenger license can be issued. The company believes that the Hong Kong government is discriminating against China. If it yields again, it will not only affect China's sovereignty and status, but will also make it impossible for China to regain its navigation rights. Therefore, it has decided to sacrifice Hong Kong passengers and use Chinese nationals as captains, refusing to take the exam.

Hong Kong Authorities Insist on Preconceived Ideas

Zhou Houkun, deputy director of the Marine Department, was specially sent to Hong Kong to negotiate with the Marine Department for the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's application for a Hong Kong passenger license for the Sihai vessel. Because the shipmaster of the Haiyuan vessel is a foreign national, there is no problem and it has already been issued. For other vessels, the Hong Kong authorities still insist on preconceived ideas. If the shipmaster is a foreigner, it can be issued, but if a Chinese is used, it is difficult to agree, and at least an examination must be added. Director Zhou repeatedly argued that the Chinese shipmaster already has a certificate issued by the Chinese government, and the Hong Kong government should not add an exam. Mr. Zhou has now returned to Shanghai on the McKinley President vessel of the Dollar Steamship Lines, saying that the Hong Kong government requires that the shipmaster, first mate, and chief engineer of the new vessel must all be foreigners before it can be granted, otherwise it will absolutely not sympathize.

Company Decides to Use Chinese Nationals

The shipmaster, first, second, and third mates of the Haiheng are all Chinese nationals. This was approved by the board of directors as early as last Thursday (as reported in this newspaper). Now, according to Director Zhou's return from Hong Kong, the Hong Kong government's position was discussed again at the board of directors. It was unanimously agreed that this matter concerns the status of the country, and the Hong Kong government is too embarrassing to China. Moreover, the shipmaster of the vessel has been appointed Ma Jiajun, and no changes will be made under any circumstances. It was decided to use Chinese nationals to drive the vessel. The chief shipmaster and the director of the Marine Department also expressed their sympathy. Therefore, the board of directors resolved that all crew members of the Haiheng vessel should be Chinese nationals and ordered them to prepare to take up their posts on the vessel immediately.

Willing to Sacrifice Hong Kong Route

However, using Chinese shipmasters, at most, will not issue passenger licenses for Hong Kong. After discussion, the company believes that the purpose of the new ocean-going vessel is specifically for Swatow and Guangdong, and it is not specifically prepared for Hong Kong passenger seats. Therefore, it is willing to sacrifice Hong Kong passengers and absolutely cannot yield to the Hong Kong authorities' demands and degrade the country's status. After this matter was announced, China's navigation industry and shipmasters expressed their admiration for the company's unyielding spirit.

Rumors of Private Takeover of the Ping-Shen Through Train 118

Neither Signed a Contract nor Registered

Chinese and Japanese Merchants Unwilling to Continue After Trial Period Expires

Japanese Side Indicates That the Two Governments Are Determined to Maintain It

The Ping-Shen through train, organized by the Oriental Travel Agency, has been in operation for nearly five months. It was once rumored that the agency would be reorganized, but then the news subsided. The agency was originally jointly established by the China Travel Service and the Japan Tourist Bureau, but recently both parties have expressed their unwillingness to continue operating it. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the New Sound News Agency specially visited the responsible personnel of both parties to inquire about the truth. The details are recorded separately below.

Chen Xiangtao's Remarks According to Chen Xiangtao, president of the China Travel Service, the organization of the Oriental Travel Agency stipulates that it must be registered with the Chinese government. Neither the China Travel Service nor the Tourist Bureau has formally signed any contract, so it has not been registered. Initially, Mr. Hirayama, the Japanese representative, drafted a contract and sent it to our representative, Zhang Shuiqi, who forwarded it to Shanghai. I instructed him to make some revisions to its contents. Then Mr. Hirayama said that it was not necessary to sign a contract for the time being. The Tourist Bureau plans to get rid of its responsibility after the trial operation period expires. Representative Zhang also stated that the China Travel Service has the same intention. This intention was originally proposed by the Japanese side. Since its establishment, the Oriental Travel Agency has handled everything on its own, and the China Travel Service has never intervened. Under these circumstances, it is unnecessary to bear the name in vain. Moreover, the China Travel Service's acceptance of the railway's entrustment is "a trial operation for six months." Therefore, the company replied to the Ministry of Railways' letter No. 2369 on June 13, which is the same opinion as the board of directors' resolution (the letter has been published). Now that the Japanese International Tourist Bureau is unwilling to continue, the company is also very willing to end it as scheduled on December 31 according to the previous board of directors' resolution. Moreover, Mr. Hirayama and Zhang Shuiqi, the persons in charge of the Oriental Travel Agency, both intend to take over in their private capacities, which the company is even more happy to see. If the Ministry of Railways still needs to continue, it will depend on the decision of the board of directors.

Tourist Bureau's Statement According to Fujisue Kenzo, manager of the Shanghai branch of the Japan International Tourist Bureau, he is not clear about the truth of the news that the bureau plans to withdraw from the Oriental Travel Agency. The truth in Shanghai has not been clarified. This matter is organized by the Tokyo headquarters, and there has been no indication to the Shanghai branch.

Attitude of the Japanese Authorities Yesterday morning, the reporter went to the Shanghai office of the Japanese Railway Ministry to inquire. Okutani Saburo, the official in charge, came out to meet. According to him, the Tourist Bureau has not made any requests to the government regarding this matter, and the officialdom has not received any formal news. He believes that this news is probably a rumor. Even if the Tourist Bureau and the China Travel Service are unwilling to continue operating it, the Chinese and Japanese governments will definitely use the power of the government to dispel this intention and continue to operate it. Furthermore, even if the Oriental Travel Agency is not continued, it is not impossible to establish another agency.

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Guild Hall has recently spared no effort in rectifying guild affairs, correcting malpractices in the industry, and seeking the welfare of the industry. Yesterday, the fifth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees of the guild hall was held. Twelve members, including Luo Qinghua, Xi Gongshi, Suo Zuosun, Cheng Weisheng, Shen Qinzhai, Wu Xingcha, Luo Liqin, Xu Limin, Lou Fengshao, Lu Zhengbing, Tu Zhongying, and Shen Jien, attended the meeting. Luo Qinghua chaired the meeting, and after performing the ceremony, the chairman reported on the reply telegram from Chairman Jiang and began to discuss (1) the case of earnestly rectifying industry regulations, which was resolved as follows: (A) The three major guidelines previously agreed upon will be submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record (B) Industry colleagues who delay in implementing the aforementioned guidelines should first be corrected by sending letters (C) Regarding the old Jiuhuo between various factories and shops, the sentiment of the host and guest between industry colleagues should be restored. After being notified in a consolidated case, letters will now be sent to all factories and shops under this guild hall to follow them together, and the Electrical Machinery Guild Hall will also be requested to forward them to its members for reference (2) The Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry plans to formulate an outline for the identification of domestic silk and satin and solicit opinions, which was resolved as follows: a letter will be sent to state opinions (3) The case of organizing a national silk exhibition, which was resolved as follows: Wang Yansong, Luo Qinghua, Wu Zhihao, Lu Zhengbing, Shen Qinzhai, Wu Xingcha, Lou Fengshao, Tu Zhongying, Luo Kunxiang, and others were appointed as preparation committee members, and a reply letter was sent to Mr. Shen Tianxin of the Hu She to jointly prepare.
